---- start moderating ----
MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because both the parties have agreed to a price of $43 and expressed satisfaction with the cooperation. The answer is Yes.

---- start bargaining ----
  seller: 很抱歉，$30的价格低于我们的最低售价。我们的保留价格是每单位$10，如果您能接受这个价格，我们可以继续讨论。
  buyer: 你会考虑以每单元$30的价格进行出售吗？
---- start moderating ----
MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because the seller offered a concession on the price and the buyer suggested a compromise regarding the delivery time. The answer is Yes.
